Headings create a hierarchy for your content.</p>\n                \n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code><span class="comment">// All six heading levels:</span>\n&lt;<span class="keyword">h1</span>&gt;Heading 1 - Main Title&lt;/<span class="keyword">h1</span>&gt;\n&lt;<span class="keyword">h2</span>&gt;Heading 2 - Sections&lt;/<span class="keyword">h2</span>&gt;\n&lt;<span class="keyword">h3</span>&gt;Heading 3 - Subsections&lt;/<span class="keyword">h3</span>&gt;\n&lt;<span class="keyword">h4</span>&gt;Heading 4 - Minor Sections&lt;/<span class="keyword">h4</span>&gt;\n&lt;<span class="keyword">h5</span>&gt;Heading 5 - Small Headings&lt;/<span class="keyword">h5</span>&gt;\n&lt;<span class="keyword">h6</span>&gt;Heading 6 - Smallest&lt;/<span class="keyword">h6</span>&gt;</code></pre>\n                </div>\n                \n                <h3>Heading Best Practices</h3>\n                <ul style="margin-left: 1.5rem; color: var(--text-gray);">\n                    <li>Use only <strong>one &lt;h1&gt;</strong> per page (the main title)</li>\n                    <li>Maintain proper hierarchy (don\'t skip from h1 to h3)</li>\n                    <li>Use headings for structure, not just to make text bigger</li>\n                    <li>Search engines use headings to understand page content</li>\n                </ul>\n                \n                <div class="tip-box">\n                    <svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg">\n                        <path d="M12 2C6.48 2 2 6.48 2 12s4.48 10 10 10 10-4.48 10-10S17.52 2 12 2zm1 15h-2v-6h2v6zm0-8h-2V7h2v2z"/>\n                    </svg>\n                    <p><strong>Semantic meaning:</strong> Headings aren\'t just about size - they tell screen readers and search engines what\'s important. A proper heading structure improves accessibility and SEO.</p>\n                </div>\n            </section>\n\n            <!-- Section 2 -->\n            <section class="lesson-section">\n                <h2>Paragraphs</h2>\n                <p>The &lt;p&gt; element defines a paragraph of text. Browsers automatically add space above and below paragraphs.</p>\n                \n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code>&lt;<span class="keyword">p</span>&gt;This is a paragraph. It contains text that will wrap \nautomatically when it reaches the edge of its container.&lt;/<span class="keyword">p</span>&gt;\n\n&lt;<span class="keyword">p</span>&gt;This is another paragraph. Each paragraph gets its own \nspacing from the one above and below it.&lt;/<span class="keyword">p</span>&gt;\n\n<span class="comment">// Output:</span>\n<span class="comment">// Two separate blocks of text with space between them</span></code></pre>\n                </div>\n                \n                <h3>White Space in HTML</h3>\n                <p>HTML collapses multiple spaces and line breaks into a single space:</p>\n                \n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code><span class="comment">// This HTML:</span>\n&lt;<span class="keyword">p</span>&gt;This    has    multiple    spaces&lt;/<span class="keyword">p</span>&gt;\n\n<span class="comment">// Displays as:</span>\nThis has multiple spaces\n\n<span class="comment">// Multiple lines also collapse:</span>\n&lt;<span class="keyword">p</span>&gt;Line one\nLine two\nLine three&lt;/<span class="keyword">p</span>&gt;\n\n<span class="comment">// Displays as:</span>\nLine one Line two Line three</code></pre>\n                </div>\n                \n                <div class="code-explanation">\n                    <p><strong>Why?</strong> HTML was designed for structure, not formatting. Use CSS to control spacing and layout, not multiple spaces or empty paragraphs.</p>\n                </div>\n            </section>\n\n            <!-- Section 3 -->\n            <section class="lesson-section">\n                <h2>Line Breaks</h2>\n                <p>Use &lt;br&gt; to create a line break within a paragraph without starting a new paragraph.</p>\n                \n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code>&lt;<span class="keyword">p</span>&gt;First line&lt;<span class="keyword">br</span>&gt;\nSecond line&lt;<span class="keyword">br</span>&gt;\nThird line&lt;/<span class="keyword">p</span>&gt;\n\n<span class="comment">// Use case: addresses, poems, lyrics</span>\n&lt;<span class="keyword">p</span>&gt;\n    123 Main Street&lt;<span class="keyword">br</span>&gt;\n    Anytown, USA 12345&lt;<span class="keyword">br</span>&gt;\n    Phone: (555) 123-4567\n&lt;/<span class="keyword">p</span>&gt;</code></pre>\n                </div>\n                \n                <div class="tip-box">\n                    <svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg">\n                        <path d="M12 2C6.48 2 2 6.48 2 12s4.48 10 10 10 10-4.48 10-10S17.52 2 12 2zm1 15h-2v-6h2v6zm0-8h-2V7h2v2z"/>\n                    </svg>\n                    <p><strong>Don\'t overuse &lt;br&gt;:</strong> It\'s meant for line breaks within content, not for creating spacing between elements. Use CSS margins for spacing.</p>\n                </div>\n            </section>\n\n            <!-- Section 4 -->\n            <section class="lesson-section">\n                <h2>Text Formatting Elements</h2>\n                <p>HTML provides elements to format text with semantic meaning:</p>\n                \n                <h3>Strong and Emphasis</h3>\n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code><span class="comment">// Strong importance (typically displays bold)</span>\n&lt;<span class="keyword">strong</span>&gt;Important text&lt;/<span class="keyword">strong</span>&gt;\n\n<span class="comment">// Emphasis (typically displays italic)</span>\n&lt;<span class="keyword">em</span>&gt;Emphasized text&lt;/<span class="keyword">em</span>&gt;\n\n<span class="comment">// Example sentence:</span>\n&lt;<span class="keyword">p</span>&gt;This is &lt;<span class="keyword">strong</span>&gt;very important&lt;/<span class="keyword">strong</span>&gt; information.&lt;/<span class="keyword">p</span>&gt;\n&lt;<span class="keyword">p</span>&gt;I &lt;<span class="keyword">em</span>&gt;really&lt;/<span class="keyword">em</span>&gt; want to go!&lt;/<span class="keyword">p</span>&gt;</code></pre>\n                </div>\n                \n                <h3>Presentation Elements (Use Sparingly)</h3>\n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code><span class="comment">// Bold text (no semantic meaning)</span>\n&lt;<span class="keyword">b</span>&gt;Bold text&lt;/<span class="keyword">b</span>&gt;\n\n<span class="comment">// Italic text (no semantic meaning)</span>\n&lt;<span class="keyword">i</span>&gt;Italic text&lt;/<span class="keyword">i</span>&gt;\n\n<span class="comment">// Underlined text</span>\n&lt;<span class="keyword">u</span>&gt;Underlined text&lt;/<span class="keyword">u</span>&gt;\n\n<span class="comment">// Strikethrough</span>\n&lt;<span class="keyword">s</span>&gt;Strikethrough text&lt;/<span class="keyword">s</span>&gt;</code></pre>\n                </div>\n                \n                <div class="code-explanation">\n                    <p><strong>Strong vs Bold:</strong> &lt;strong&gt; means "this is important" (semantic). &lt;b&gt; just means "make this bold" (presentational). Use &lt;strong&gt; for accessibility - screen readers may announce it differently.</p>\n                </div>\n            </section>\n\n            <!-- Section 5 -->\n            <section class="lesson-section">\n                <h2>Other Text Elements</h2>\n                \n                <h3>Mark (Highlight)</h3>\n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code>&lt;<span class="keyword">p</span>&gt;This is &lt;<span class="keyword">mark</span>&gt;highlighted text&lt;/<span class="keyword">mark</span>&gt;.&lt;/<span class="keyword">p</span>&gt;</code></pre>\n                </div>\n                \n                <h3>Small</h3>\n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code>&lt;<span class="keyword">p</span>&gt;&lt;<span class="keyword">small</span>&gt;Terms and conditions apply.&lt;/<span class="keyword">small</span>&gt;&lt;/<span class="keyword">p</span>&gt;</code></pre>\n                </div>\n                \n                <h3>Subscript and Superscript</h3>\n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code><span class="comment">// Subscript (below baseline)</span>\nH&lt;<span class="keyword">sub</span>&gt;2&lt;/<span class="keyword">sub</span>&gt;O    <span class="comment">// Water formula</span>\n\n<span class="comment">// Superscript (above baseline)</span>\nE = mc&lt;<span class="keyword">sup</span>&gt;2&lt;/<span class="keyword">sup</span>&gt;    <span class="comment">// Einstein\'s equation</span>\n1&lt;<span class="keyword">sup</span>&gt;st&lt;/<span class="keyword">sup</span&gt; 2&lt;<span class="keyword">sup</span>&gt;nd&lt;/<span class="keyword">sup</span>&gt; 3&lt;<span class="keyword">sup</span>&gt;rd&lt;/<span class="keyword">sup</span>&gt;    <span class="comment">// Ordinal numbers</span></code></pre>\n                </div>\n                \n                <h3>Code Elements</h3>\n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code><span class="comment">// Inline code</span>\n&lt;<span class="keyword">p</span>&gt;Use the &lt;<span class="keyword">code</span>&gt;console.log()&lt;/<span class="keyword">code</span>&gt; function.&lt;/<span class="keyword">p</span>&gt;\n\n<span class="comment">// Preformatted text (preserves spaces and line breaks)</span>\n&lt;<span class="keyword">pre</span>&gt;\nfunction greet() {\n    console.log("Hello!");\n}\n&lt;/<span class="keyword">pre</span>&gt;\n\n<span class="comment">// Keyboard input</span>\n&lt;<span class="keyword">p</span>&gt;Press &lt;<span class="keyword">kbd</span>&gt;Ctrl&lt;/<span class="keyword">kbd</span>&gt; + &lt;<span class="keyword">kbd</span>&gt;C&lt;/<span class="keyword">kbd</span>&gt; to copy.&lt;/<span class="keyword">p</span>&gt;</code></pre>\n                </div>\n            </section>\n\n            <!-- Section 6 -->\n            <section class="lesson-section">\n                <h2>Blockquote and Quote</h2>\n                \n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code><span class="comment">// Blockquote (for longer quotes)</span>\n&lt;<span class="keyword">blockquote</span>&gt;\n    &lt;<span class="keyword">p</span>&gt;The only way to do great work is to love what you do.&lt;/<span class="keyword">p</span>&gt;\n    &lt;<span class="keyword">footer</span>&gt;— Steve Jobs&lt;/<span class="keyword">footer</span>&gt;\n&lt;/<span class="keyword">blockquote</span>&gt;\n\n<span class="comment">// Inline quote</span>\n&lt;<span class="keyword">p</span>&gt;He said, &lt;<span class="keyword">q</span>&gt;Hello, world!&lt;/<span class="keyword">q</span>&gt; and smiled.&lt;/<span class="keyword">p</span>&gt;\n\n<span class="comment">// With citation</span>\n&lt;<span class="keyword">blockquote</span> <span class="variable">cite</span>=<span class="string">"https://example.com/quote-source"</span>&gt;\n    &lt;<span class="keyword">p</span>&gt;A famous quote here.&lt;/<span class="keyword">p</span>&gt;\n&lt;/<span class="keyword">blockquote</span>&gt;</code></pre>\n                </div>\n            </section>\n\n            <!-- Section 7 -->\n            <section class="lesson-section">\n                <h2>Horizontal Rule</h2>\n                <p>The &lt;hr&gt; element creates a thematic break between sections.</p>\n                \n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code>&lt;<span class="keyword">h2</span>&gt;Chapter 1&lt;/<span class="keyword">h2</span>&gt;\n&lt;<span class="keyword">p</span>&gt;Content of chapter 1...&lt;/<span class="keyword">p</span>&gt;\n\n&lt;<span class="keyword">hr</span>&gt;\n\n&lt;<span class="keyword">h2</span>&gt;Chapter 2&lt;/<span class="keyword">h2</span>&gt;\n&lt;<span class="keyword">p</span>&gt;Content of chapter 2...&lt;/<span class="keyword">p</span>&gt;</code></pre>\n                </div>\n                \n                <div class="code-explanation">\n                    <p><strong>Semantic meaning:</strong> &lt;hr&gt; isn\'t just a visual line - it represents a thematic change in content, like a scene change in a story or a transition to a new topic.</p>\n                </div>\n            </section>\n\n            <!-- Key Takeaways -->\n            <section class="lesson-section">\n                <h2>Key Takeaways</h2>\n                <div class="tip-box">\n                    <svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg">\n                        <path d="M12 2C6.48 2 2 6.48 2 12s4.48 10 10 10 10-4.48 10-10S17.52 2 12 2zm1 15h-2v-6h2v6zm0-8h-2V7h2v2z"/>\n                    </svg>\n                    <div>\n                        <p><strong>Remember:</strong></p>\n                        <ul style="margin-top: 0.5rem; margin-left: 1.5rem;">\n                            <li><strong>&lt;h1&gt;-&lt;h6&gt;:</strong> Use for headings, only one h1 per page</li>\n                            <li><strong>&lt;p&gt;:</strong> For paragraphs of text</li>\n                            <li><strong>&lt;br&gt;:</strong> Line break within text</li>\n                            <li><strong>&lt;strong&gt;:</strong> Important text (semantic)</li>\n                            <li><strong>&lt;em&gt;:</strong> Emphasized text (semantic)</li>\n                            <li><strong>&lt;code&gt;:</strong> Inline code snippets</li>\n                            <li><strong>&lt;pre&gt;:</strong> Preserves formatting and whitespace</li>\n                            <li><strong>Semantic elements:</strong> Add meaning, not just style</li>\n                        </ul>\n                    </div>\n                </div>\n            </section>\n\n            <!-- Navigation -->\n            <div class="nav-buttons">\n                <a href="lesson2.html" class="nav-btn prev">← Previous: Document Structure</a>\n                <a href="lesson4.html" class="nav-btn next">Next: Links and Images →</a>\n            </div>\n        </div>\n    </main>\n\n    <!-- Footer -->\n    <footer class="footer">\n        <p>© 2024 Learner. page.</p>\n                \n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code><span class="comment">// Basic link syntax:</span>\n&lt;<span class="keyword">a</span> <span external sites:</p>\n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code><span class="comment">// Link to another website</span>\n&lt;<span class="keyword">a</span> <span class="variable">href</span>=<span class="string">"https://www.google.com"</span>&gt;Go to Google&lt;/<span class="keyword">a</span>&gt;\n\n<span class="comment">// Link to a specific page</span>\n&lt;<span class="keyword">a</span> <span class="variable">href</span>=<span class="string">"https://example.com/about"</span>&gt;About Us&lt;/<span class="keyword">a</span>&gt;</code></pre>\n                </div>\n                \n                <h3>Relative URLs</h3>\n                <p>Links to pages within your own website:</p>\n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code><span class="comment">// Same folder</span>\n&lt;<span class="keyword">a</span> <span class="variable">href</span>=<span class="string">"about.html"</span>&gt;About&lt;/<span class="keyword">a</span>&gt;\n\n<span class="comment">// Subfolder</span>\n&lt;<span class="keyword">a</span> <span level)</span>\n&lt;<span class="keyword">a</span> <span class="variable">href</span>=<span class="string">"../index.html"</span>&gt;Home&lt;/<span class="keyword">a</span>&gt;\n\n<span class="comment">// Root-relative (starts from website root)</span>\n&lt;<span class="keyword">a</span> <span class="variable">href</span>=<span          <h2>Link Targets</h2>\n                <p>The <code>target</code> attribute controls where the link opens:</p>\n                \n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code><span class="comment">// Open in same tab (default)</span>\n&lt;<span class="keyword">a</span> <span class="variable">href</span>=<span class="string">"https://example.com"</span>&gt;Same tab&lt;/<span class="keyword">a</span>&gt;\n\n<span class="comment">// Open in new tab/window</span>\n&lt;<span class="keyword">a</span> <span class="variable">href</span>=<span class="string">"https://example.com"</span> <span class="variable">target</span>=<span class="string">"_blank"</span>&gt;New tab&lt;/<span class="keyword">a</span>&gt;\n\n<span class="comment">// Security best practice for external links:</span>\n&lt;<span class="keyword">a</span> <span class="variable">href</span>=<span class="string">"https://example.com"</span> \n   <span class="variable">target</span>=<span class="string">"_blank"</span> \n   <span class="variable">rel</span>=<span class="string">"noopener noreferrer"</span>&gt;\n    Safe external link\n&lt;/<span class="keyword">a</span>&gt;</code></pre>\n                </div>\n                \n                <div class="tip-box">\n                    <svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg">\n                        <path d="M12 2C6.48 2 2 6.48 2 12s4.48 10 10 10 10-4.48 10-10S17.52 2 12 2zm1 15h-2v-6h2v6zm0-8h-2V7h2v2z"/>\n                    </svg>\n                    <p><strong>Security tip:</strong> Always add <code>rel="noopener noreferrer"</code> to external links with <code>target="_blank"</code>. This prevents the linked page from accessing your page\'s window object.</p>\n                </div>\n            </section>\n\n            <!-- Section 4 -->\n            <section class="lesson-section">\n                <h2>Other Link Types</h2>\n                \n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code><span class="comment">// Email link (opens email client)</span>\n&lt;<span class="keyword">a</span> <span class="variable">href</span>=<span class="string">"mailto:someone@example.com"</span>&gt;Send Email&lt;/<span class="keyword">a</span>&gt;\n\n<span class="comment">// Email with subject and body</span>\n&lt;<span class="keyword">a</span> <span class="variable">href</span>=<span class="string">"mailto:someone@example.com?subject=Hello&amp;body=Hi there"</span>&gt;\n    Send Email\n&lt;/<span class="keyword">a</span>&gt;\n\n<span class="comment">// Phone number (useful on mobile)</span>\n&lt;<span class="keyword">a</span> <span class="variable">href</span>=<span class="string">"tel:+1234567890"</span>&gt;Call Us&lt;/<span class="keyword">a</span>&gt;\n\n<span class="comment">// Download link</span>\n&lt;<span class="keyword">a</span> <span class="variable">href</span>=<span class="string">"files/document.pdf"</span> <span class="variable">download</span>&gt;Download PDF&lt;/<span class="keyword">a</span>&gt;\n\n<span class="comment">// Download with custom filename</span>\n&lt;<span class="keyword">a</span> <span class="variable">href</span>=<span class="string">"files/doc.pdf"</span> <span class="variable">download</span>=<span class="string">"my-document.pdf"</span>&gt;Download&lt;/<span class="keyword">a</span>&gt;</code></pre>\n                </div>\n            </section>\n\n            <!-- Section 5 -->\n            <section class="lesson-section">\n                <h2>Images</h2>\n                <p>The &lt;img&gt; element embeds images in your page. It\'s a self-closing tag.</p>\n                \n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code><span class="comment">// Basic image syntax:</span>\n&lt;<span class="keyword">img</span> <span class="variable">src</span>=<span class="string">"photo.jpg"</span> <span class="variable">alt</span>=<span class="string">"Description of image"</span>&gt;\n     ↑                ↑\n   source          alternative text\n   (required)      (required for accessibility)</code></pre>\n                </div>\n                \n                <h3>Required Attributes</h3>\n                <ul style="margin-left: 1.5rem; color: var(--text-gray);">\n                    <li><strong>src:</strong> The path to the image file (URL or file path)</li>\n                    <li><strong>alt:</strong> Alternative text describing the image (for accessibility and when image fails to load)</li>\n                </ul>\n                \n                <div class="tip-box">\n                    <svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg">\n                        <path d="M12 2C6.48 2 2 6.48 2 12s4.48 10 10 10 10-4.48 10-10S17.52 2 12 2zm1 15h-2v-6h2v6zm0-8h-2V7h2v2z"/>\n                    </svg>\n                    <p><strong>Alt text is crucial!</strong> Screen readers use it to describe images to visually impaired users. It also displays if the image fails to load and helps search engines understand the image content.</p>\n                </div>\n            </section>\n\n            <!-- Section 6 -->\n            <section class="lesson-section">\n                <h2>Image Sizing</h2>\n                \n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code><span class="comment">// Set width and height (in pixels)</span>\n&lt;<span class="keyword">img</span> <span class="variable">src</span>=<span class="string">"photo.jpg"</span> \n     <span class="variable">alt</span>=<span class="string">"A sunset"</span> \n     <span class="variable">width</span>=<span class="string">"300"</span> \n     <span class="variable">height</span>=<span class="string">"200"</span>&gt;\n\n<span class="comment">// Or use CSS for responsive images</span>\n&lt;<span class="keyword">img</span> <span class="variable">src</span>=<span class="string">"photo.jpg"</span> \n     <span class="variable">alt</span>=<span class="string">"A sunset"</span> \n     <span class="variable">style</span>=<span class="string">"width: 100%; max-width: 500px;"</span>&gt;</code></pre>\n                </div>\n                \n                <div class="code-explanation">\n                    <p><strong>Best practice:</strong> Always specify width and height attributes to prevent layout shift while the image loads. Use CSS for responsive sizing.</p>\n                </div>\n            </section>\n\n            <!-- Section 7 -->\n            <section class="lesson-section">\n                <h2>Image Paths</h2>\n                \n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code><span class="comment">// Image in same folder as HTML file</span>\n&lt;<span class="keyword">img</span> <span class="variable">src</span>=<span class="string">"photo.jpg"</span> <span class="variable">alt</span>=<span class="string">"Photo"</span>&gt;\n\n<span class="comment">// Image in a subfolder</span>\n&lt;<span class="keyword">img</span> <span class="variable">src</span>=<span class="string">"images/photo.jpg"</span> <span class="variable">alt</span>=<span class="string">"Photo"</span>&gt;\n\n<span class="comment">// Image in parent folder</span>\n&lt;<span class="keyword">img</span> <span class="variable">src</span>=<span class="string">"../photo.jpg"</span> <span class="variable">alt</span>=<span class="string">"Photo"</span>&gt;\n\n<span class="comment">// Image from another website (absolute URL)</span>\n&lt;<span class="keyword">img</span> <span class="variable">src</span>=<span class="string">"https://example.com/images/photo.jpg"</span> <span class="variable">alt</span>=<span class="string">"Photo"</span>&gt;</code></pre>\n                </div>\n            </section>\n\n            <!-- Section 8 -->\n            <section class="lesson-section">\n                <h2>Image Formats</h2>\n                <p>Common image formats for the web:</p>\n                \n                <ul style="margin-left: 1.5rem; color: var(--text-gray);">\n                    <li><strong>JPEG (.jpg):</strong> Photos and complex images with many colors</li>\n                    <li><strong>PNG (.png):</strong> Images with transparency, logos, icons</li>\n                    <li><strong>GIF (.gif):</strong> Simple animations, limited colors</li>\n                    <li><strong>WebP (.webp):</strong> Modern format with better compression</li>\n                    <li><strong>SVG (.svg):</strong> Vector graphics, logos, icons (scales perfectly)</li>\n                </ul>\n            </section>\n\n            <!-- Section 9 -->\n            <section class="lesson-section">\n                <h2>Images as Links</h2>\n                <p>Wrap an image in an anchor tag to make it clickable:</p>\n                \n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code><span class="comment">// Clickable image</span>\n&lt;<span class="keyword">a</span> <span class="variable">href</span>=<span class="string">"https://example.com"</span>&gt;\n    &lt;<span class="keyword">img</span> <span class="variable">src</span>=<span class="string">"logo.png"</span> <span class="variable">alt</span>=<span class="string">"Company Logo"</span>&gt;\n&lt;/<span class="keyword">a</span>&gt;\n\n<span class="comment">// Common for logos that link to homepage</span></code></pre>\n                </div>\n            </section>\n\n            <!-- Section 10 -->\n            <section class="lesson-section">\n                <h2>Figure and Figcaption</h2>\n                <p>Semantic elements for images with captions:</p>\n                \n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code>&lt;<span class="keyword">figure</span>&gt;\n    &lt;<span class="keyword">img</span> <span class="variable">src</span>=<span class="string">"sunset.jpg"</span> <span class="variable">alt</span>=<span class="string">"A beautiful sunset over the ocean"</span>&gt;\n    &lt;<span class="keyword">figcaption</span>&gt;Photo taken at Malibu Beach, California&lt;/<span class="keyword">figcaption</span>&gt;\n&lt;/<span class="keyword">figure</span>&gt;\n\n<span class="comment">// &lt;figure&gt;: Container for self-contained content</span>\n<span class="comment">// &lt;figcaption&gt;: Caption or description for the figure</span></code></pre>\n                </div>\n            </section>\n\n            <!-- Key Takeaways -->\n            <section class="lesson-section">\n                <h2>Key Takeaways</h2>\n                <div class="tip-box">\n                    <svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg">\n                        <path d="M12 2C6.48 2 2 6.48 2 12s4.48 10 10 10 10-4.48 10-10S17.52 2 12 2zm1 15h-2v-6h2v6zm0-8h-2V7h2v2z"/>\n                    </svg>\n                    <div>\n                        <p><strong>Remember:</strong></p>\n                        <ul style="margin-top: 0.5rem; margin-left: 1.5rem;">\n                            <li><strong>&lt;a href=""&gt;:</strong> Creates links to other pages or resources</li>\n                            <li><strong>Relative URLs:</strong> For internal links within your site</li>\n                            <li><strong>Absolute URLs:</strong> For external links to other websites</li>\n                            <li><strong>target="_blank":</strong> Opens link in new tab</li>\n                            <li><strong>&lt;img src="" alt=""&gt;:</strong> Embeds images</li>\n                            <li><strong>alt attribute:</strong> Essential for accessibility</li>\n                            <li><strong>width/height:</strong> Prevents layout shift</li>\n                            <li><strong>&lt;figure&gt;/&lt;figcaption&gt;:</strong> Semantic image with caption</li>\n                        </ul>\n                    </div>\n                </div>\n            </section>\n\n            <!-- Navigation -->\n            <div class="nav-buttons">\n                <a href="lesson3.html" for numbered lists where order matters:</p>\n                \n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code>&lt;<span class="keyword">ol</span>&gt;\n    &lt;<span class="keyword">li</span>&gt;First item&lt;/<span class="keyword">li</span>&gt;\n    &lt;<span class="keyword">li</span>&gt;Second item&lt;/<span class="keyword">li</span>&gt;\n    &lt;<span class="keyword">li</span>&gt;Third item&lt;/<span class="keyword">li</span>&gt;\n&lt;/<span class="keyword">ol</span>&gt;\n\n<span class="comment">// Output:</span>\n<span class="number">1.</span> First item\n<span class="number">2.</span> Second item\n<span class="number">3.</span> Third item\n\n<span class="comment">// Each item is wrapped in &lt;li&gt; (list item)</span></code></pre>\n                </div>\n                \n                <h3>Ordered List Attributes</h3>\n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code><span class="comment">// Change numbering type</span>\n&lt;<span class="keyword">ol</span> <span class="variable">type</span>=<span class="string">"A"</span>&gt;        <span class="comment">// A, B, C...</span>\n&lt;<span class="keyword">ol</span> <span class="variable">type</span>=<span class="string">"a"</span>&gt;        <span class="comment">// a, b, c...</span>\n&lt;<span class="keyword">ol</span> <span class="variable">type</span>=<span class="string">"I"</span>&gt;        <span class="comment">// I, II, III...</span>\n&lt;<span class="keyword">ol</span> <span class="variable">type</span>=<span class="string">"i"</span>&gt;        <span class="comment">// i, ii, iii...</span>\n&lt;<span class="keyword">ol</span> <span class="variable">type</span>=<span class="string">"1"</span>&gt;        <span class="comment">// 1, 2, 3... (default)</span>\n\n<span class="comment">// Start from a different number</span>\n&lt;<span class="keyword">ol</span> <span class="variable">start</span>=<span class="string">"5"</span>&gt;\n    &lt;<span class="keyword">li</span>&gt;This is item 5&lt;/<span class="keyword">li</span>&gt;\n    &lt;<span class="keyword">li</span>&gt;This is item 6&lt;/<span class="keyword">li</span>&gt;\n&lt;/<span class="keyword">ol</span>&gt;\n\n<span class="comment">// Reverse the order</span>\n&lt;<span class="keyword">ol</span> <span class="variable">reversed</span>&gt;\n    &lt;<span class="keyword">li</span>&gt;Third&lt;/<span class="keyword">li</span>&gt;\n    &lt;<span class="keyword">li</span>&gt;Second&lt;/<span class="keyword">li</span>&gt;\n    &lt;<span class="keyword">li</span>&gt;First&lt;/<span class="keyword">li</span>&gt;\n&lt;/<span class="keyword">ol</span>&gt;</code></pre>\n                </div>\n            </section>\n\n            <!-- Section 2 -->\n            <section class="lesson-section">\n                <h2>Unordered Lists</h2>\n                <p>Use &lt;ul&gt; for bullet-point lists where order doesn\'t matter:</p>\n                \n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code>&lt;<span class="keyword">ul</span>&gt;\n    &lt;<span class="keyword">li</span>&gt;Apples&lt;/<span class="keyword">li</span>&gt;\n    &lt;<span class="keyword">li</span>&gt;Oranges&lt;/<span class="keyword">li</span>&gt;\n    &lt;<span class="keyword">li</span>&gt;Bananas&lt;/<span class="keyword">li</span>&gt;\n&lt;/<span class="keyword">ul</span>&gt;\n\n<span class="comment">// Output:</span>\n• Apples\n• Oranges\n• Bananas</code></pre>\n                </div>\n                \n                <h3>Changing Bullet Style (with CSS)</h3>\n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code><span class="comment">// CSS controls bullet style:</span>\n&lt;<span class="keyword">ul</span> <span class="variable">style</span>=<span class="string">"list-style-type: disc;"</span>&gt;    <span class="comment">// • (default)</span>\n&lt;<span class="keyword">ul</span> <span class="variable">style</span>=<span class="string">"list-style-type: circle;"</span>&gt;  <span class="comment">// ○</span>\n&lt;<span class="keyword">ul</span> <span class="variable">style</span>=<span class="string">"list-style-type: square;"</span>&gt;  <span class="comment">// ■</span>\n&lt;<span class="keyword">ul</span> <span class="variable">style</span>=<span class="string">"list-style-type: none;"</span>&gt;    <span class="comment">// No bullets</span></code></pre>\n                </div>\n            </section>\n\n            <!-- Section 3 -->\n            <section class="lesson-section">\n                <h2>Nested Lists</h2>\n                <p>Lists can be nested inside other lists:</p>\n                \n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code>&lt;<span class="keyword">ul</span>&gt;\n    &lt;<span class="keyword">li</span>&gt;Fruits\n        &lt;<span class="keyword">ul</span>&gt;\n            &lt;<span class="keyword">li</span>&gt;Apples&lt;/<span class="keyword">li</span>&gt;\n            &lt;<span class="keyword">li</span>&gt;Oranges&lt;/<span class="keyword">li</span>&gt;\n        &lt;/<span class="keyword">ul</span>&gt;\n    &lt;/<span class="keyword">li</span>&gt;\n    &lt;<span class="keyword">li</span>&gt;Vegetables\n        &lt;<span class="keyword">ul</span>&gt;\n            &lt;<span class="keyword">li</span>&gt;Carrots&lt;/<span class="keyword">li</span>&gt;\n            &lt;<span class="keyword">li</span>&gt;Broccoli&lt;/<span class="keyword">li</span>&gt;\n        &lt;/<span class="keyword">ul</span>&gt;\n    &lt;/<span class="keyword">li</span>&gt;\n&lt;/<span class="keyword">ul</span>&gt;\n\n<span class="comment">// Output:</span>\n• Fruits\n    ○ Apples\n    ○ Oranges\n• Vegetables\n    ○ Carrots\n    ○ Broccoli</code></pre>\n                </div>\n                \n                <div class="tip-box">\n                    <svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg">\n                        <path d="M12 2C6.48 2 2 6.48 2 12s4.48 10 10 10 10-4.48 10-10S17.52 2 12 2zm1 15h-2v-6h2v6zm0-8h-2V7h2v2z"/>\n                    </svg>\n                    <p><strong>Important:</strong> Nested lists must be inside an &lt;li&gt; element, not directly inside another list element.</p>\n                </div>\n            </section>\n\n            <!-- Section 4 -->\n            <section class="lesson-section">\n                <h2>Description Lists</h2>\n                <p>Use &lt;dl&gt; for lists with terms and descriptions:</p>\n                \n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code>&lt;<span class="keyword">dl</span>&gt;\n    &lt;<span class="keyword">dt</span>&gt;HTML&lt;/<span class="keyword">dt</span>&gt;\n    &lt;<span class="keyword">dd</span>&gt;HyperText Markup Language - the structure of web pages&lt;/<span class="keyword">dd</span>&gt;\n    \n    &lt;<span class="keyword">dt</span>&gt;CSS&lt;/<span class="keyword">dt</span>&gt;\n    &lt;<span class="keyword">dd</span>&gt;Cascading Style Sheets - styling for web pages&lt;/<span class="keyword">dd</span>&gt;\n    \n    &lt;<span class="keyword">dt</span>&gt;JavaScript&lt;/<span class="keyword">dt</span>&gt;\n    &lt;<span class="keyword">dd</span>&gt;A programming language for interactive web pages&lt;/<span class="keyword">dd</span>&gt;\n&lt;/<span class="keyword">dl</span>&gt;\n\n<span class="comment">// dt = description term</span>\n<span class="comment">// dd = description details</span></code></pre>\n                </div>\n            </section>\n\n            <!-- Section 5 -->\n            <section class="lesson-section">\n                <h2>Basic Table Structure</h2>\n                <p>Tables organize data in rows and columns:</p>\n                \n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code>&lt;<span class="keyword">table</span>&gt;\n    &lt;<span class="keyword">tr</span>&gt;                          <span class="comment">// Table row</span>\n        &lt;<span class="keyword">th</span>&gt;Name&lt;/<span class="keyword">th</span>&gt;              <span class="comment">// Table header cell</span>\n        &lt;<span class="keyword">th</span>&gt;Age&lt;/<span class="keyword">th</span>&gt;\n        &lt;<span class="keyword">th</span>&gt;City&lt;/<span class="keyword">th</span>&gt;\n    &lt;/<span class="keyword">tr</span>&gt;\n    &lt;<span class="keyword">tr</span>&gt;\n        &lt;<span class="keyword">td</span>&gt;John&lt;/<span class="keyword">td</span>&gt;             <span class="comment">// Table data cell</span>\n        &lt;<span class="keyword">td</span>&gt;25&lt;/<span class="keyword">td</span>&gt;\n        &lt;<span class="keyword">td</span>&gt;New York&lt;/<span class="keyword">td</span>&gt;\n    &lt;/<span class="keyword">tr</span>&gt;\n    &lt;<span class="keyword">tr</span>&gt;\n        &lt;<span class="keyword">td</span>&gt;Jane&lt;/<span class="keyword">td</span>&gt;\n        &lt;<span class="keyword">td</span>&gt;30&lt;/<span class="keyword">td</span>&gt;\n        &lt;<span class="keyword">td</span>&gt;Los Angeles&lt;/<span class="keyword">td</span>&gt;\n    &lt;/<span class="keyword">tr</span>&gt;\n&lt;/<span class="keyword">table</span>&gt;</code></pre>\n                </div>\n                \n                <div class="code-explanation">\n                    <p><strong>Table elements:</strong><br>\n                    &lt;table&gt; - Container for the entire table<br>\n                    &lt;tr&gt; - Table row<br>\n                    &lt;th&gt; - Table header (bold, centered by default)<br>\n                    &lt;td&gt; - Table data (regular cell)</p>\n                </div>\n            </section>\n\n            <!-- Section 6 -->\n            <section class="lesson-section">\n                <h2>Table Sections</h2>\n                <p>Organize tables into logical sections:</p>\n                \n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code>&lt;<span class="keyword">table</span>&gt;\n    &lt;<span class="keyword">thead</span>&gt;                      <span class="comment">// Table head section</span>\n        &lt;<span class="keyword">tr</span>&gt;\n            &lt;<span class="keyword">th</span>&gt;Name&lt;/<span class="keyword">th</span>&gt;\n            &lt;<span class="keyword">th</span>&gt;Score&lt;/<span class="keyword">th</span>&gt;\n        &lt;/<span class="keyword">tr</span>&gt;\n    &lt;/<span class="keyword">thead</span>&gt;\n    &lt;<span class="keyword">tbody</span>&gt;                      <span class="comment">// Table body section</span>\n        &lt;<span class="keyword">tr</span>&gt;\n            &lt;<span class="keyword">td</span>&gt;Alice&lt;/<span class="keyword">td</span>&gt;\n            &lt;<span class="keyword">td</span>&gt;95&lt;/<span class="keyword">td</span>&gt;\n        &lt;/<span class="keyword">tr</span>&gt;\n        &lt;<span class="keyword">tr</span>&gt;\n            &lt;<span class="keyword">td</span>&gt;Bob&lt;/<span class="keyword">td</span>&gt;\n            &lt;<span class="keyword">td</span>&gt;87&lt;/<span class="keyword">td</span>&gt;\n        &lt;/<span class="keyword">tr</span>&gt;\n    &lt;/<span class="keyword">tbody</span>&gt;\n    &lt;<span class="keyword">tfoot</span>&gt;                      <span class="comment">// Table footer section</span>\n        &lt;<span class="keyword">tr</span>&gt;\n            &lt;<span class="keyword">td</span>&gt;Average&lt;/<span class="keyword">td</span>&gt;\n            &lt;<span class="keyword">td</span>&gt;91&lt;/<span class="keyword">td</span>&gt;\n        &lt;/<span class="keyword">tr</span>&gt;\n    &lt;/<span class="keyword">tfoot</span>&gt;\n&lt;/<span class="keyword">table</span>&gt;</code></pre>\n                </div>\n                \n                <div class="tip-box">\n                    <svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg">\n                        <path d="M12 2C6.48 2 2 6.48 2 12s4.48 10 10 10 10-4.48 10-10S17.52 2 12 2zm1 15h-2v-6h2v6zm0-8h-2V7h2v2z"/>\n                    </svg>\n                    <p><strong>Why use sections?</strong> They improve accessibility, help with printing (header repeats on each page), and make styling easier with CSS.</p>\n                </div>\n            </section>\n\n            <!-- Section 7 -->\n            <section class="lesson-section">\n                <h2>Spanning Rows and Columns</h2>\n                <p>Cells can span multiple rows or columns:</p>\n                \n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code>&lt;<span class="keyword">table</span>&gt;\n    &lt;<span class="keyword">tr</span>&gt;\n        &lt;<span class="keyword">th</span> <span class="variable">colspan</span>=<span class="string">"3"</span>&gt;Quarterly Report&lt;/<span class="keyword">th</span>&gt;  <span class="comment">// Spans 3 columns</span>\n    &lt;/<span class="keyword">tr</span>&gt;\n    &lt;<span class="keyword">tr</span>&gt;\n        &lt;<span class="keyword">th</span>&gt;Q1&lt;/<span class="keyword">th</span>&gt;\n        &lt;<span class="keyword">th</span>&gt;Q2&lt;/<span class="keyword">th</span>&gt;\n        &lt;<span class="keyword">th</span>&gt;Q3&lt;/<span class="keyword">th</span>&gt;\n    &lt;/<span class="keyword">tr</span>&gt;\n    &lt;<span class="keyword">tr</span>&gt;\n        &lt;<span class="keyword">td</span> <span class="variable">rowspan</span>=<span class="string">"2"</span>&gt;Sales&lt;/<span class="keyword">td</span>&gt;    <span class="comment">// Spans 2 rows</span>\n        &lt;<span class="keyword">td</span>&gt;$1000&lt;/<span class="keyword">td</span>&gt;\n        &lt;<span class="keyword">td</span>&gt;$1200&lt;/<span class="keyword">td</span>&gt;\n    &lt;/<span class="keyword">tr</span>&gt;\n    &lt;<span class="keyword">tr</span>&gt;\n        &lt;<span class="keyword">td</span>&gt;$1100&lt;/<span class="keyword">td</span>&gt;\n        &lt;<span class="keyword">td</span>&gt;$1300&lt;/<span class="keyword">td</span>&gt;\n    &lt;/<span class="keyword">tr</span>&gt;\n&lt;/<span class="keyword">table</span>&gt;</code></pre>\n                </div>\n            </section>\n\n            <!-- Section 8 -->\n            <section class="lesson-section">\n                <h2>Table Caption</h2>\n                <p>Add a title to your table:</p>\n                \n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code>&lt;<span class="keyword">table</span>&gt;\n    &lt;<span class="keyword">caption</span>&gt;Monthly Sales Report&lt;/<span class="keyword">caption</span>&gt;\n    &lt;<span class="keyword">thead</span>&gt;\n        &lt;<span class="keyword">tr</span>&gt;\n            &lt;<span class="keyword">th</span>&gt;Month&lt;/<span class="keyword">th</span>&gt;\n            &lt;<span class="keyword">th</span>&gt;Sales&lt;/<span class="keyword">th</span>&gt;\n        &lt;/<span class="keyword">tr</span>&gt;\n    &lt;/<span class="keyword">thead</span>&gt;\n    <span class="comment">// ... more rows</span>\n&lt;/<span class="keyword">table</span>&gt;</code></pre>\n                </div>\n            </section>\n\n            <!-- Key Takeaways -->\n            <section class="lesson-section">\n                <h2>Key Takeaways</h2>\n                <div class="tip-box">\n                    <svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg">\n                        <path d="M12 2C6.48 2 2 6.48 2 12s4.48 10 10 10 10-4.48 10-10S17.52 2 12 2zm1 15h-2v-6h2v6zm0-8h-2V7h2v2z"/>\n                    </svg>\n                    <div>\n                        <p><strong>Remember:</strong></p>\n                        <ul style="margin-top: 0.5rem; margin-left: 1.5rem;">\n                            <li><strong>&lt;ol&gt;:</strong> Ordered (numbered) lists</li>\n                            <li><strong>&lt;ul&gt;:</strong> Unordered (bulleted) lists</li>\n                            <li><strong>&lt;li&gt;:</strong> List item (inside ol or ul)</li>\n                            <li><strong>&lt;dl&gt;/&lt;dt&gt;/&lt;dd&gt;:</strong> Description lists</li>\n                            <li><strong>&lt;table&gt;:</strong> Container for tables</li>\n                            <li><strong>&lt;tr&gt;:</strong> Table row</li>\n                            <li><strong>&lt;th&gt;:</strong> Table header cell</li>\n                            <li><strong>&lt;td&gt;:</strong> Table data cell</li>\n                            <li><strong>colspan/rowspan:</strong> Merge cells across columns/rows</li>\n                            <li><strong>&lt;thead&gt;/&lt;tbody&gt;/&lt;tfoot&gt;:</strong> Logical table sections</li>\n                        </ul>\n                    </div>\n                </div>\n            </section>\n\n            <!-- Navigation -->\n            <div class="nav-buttons">\n                <a          <section class="lesson-section">\n                <h2>The Form Element</h2>\n                <p>The &lt;form&gt; element is a container for all the inputs that collect user data.</p>\n                \n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code>&lt;<span class="keyword">form</span> <span class="variable">action</span>=<span class="string">"/submit"</span> <span class="variable">method</span>=<span class="string">"POST"</span>&gt;\n    <span class="comment">// Form inputs go here</span>\n&lt;/<span class="keyword">form</span>&gt;\n\n<span class="comment">// action: Where to send the data (URL)</span>\n<span class="comment">// method: How to send it (GET or POST)</span>\n\n<span class="comment">// GET: Data visible in URL (search, filters)</span>\n<span class="comment">// POST: Data hidden in request body (login, forms)</span></code></pre>\n                </div>\n            </section>\n\n            <!-- Section 2 -->\n            <section class="lesson-section">\n                <h2>Text Inputs</h2>\n                <p>The most common input type for collecting text:</p>\n                \n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code><span class="comment">// Basic text input</span>\n&lt;<span class="keyword">input</span> <span class="variable">type</span>=<span class="string">"text"</span> <span class="variable">name</span>=<span class="string">"username"</span>&gt;\n\n<span class="comment">// With label (important for accessibility)</span>\n&lt;<span class="keyword">label</span> <span class="variable">for</span>=<span class="string">"username"</span>&gt;Username:&lt;/<span class="keyword">label</span>&gt;\n&lt;<span class="keyword">input</span> <span class="variable">type</span>=<span class="string">"text"</span> <span class="variable">id</span>=<span class="string">"username"</span> <span class="variable">name</span>=<span class="string">"username"</span>&gt;\n\n<span class="comment">// With placeholder and required</span>\n&lt;<span class="keyword">input</span> <span class="variable">type</span>=<span class="string">"text"</span> \n       <span class="variable">name</span>=<span class="string">"username"</span> \n       <span class="variable">placeholder</span>=<span class="string">"Enter your username"</span>\n       <span class="variable">required</span>&gt;\n\n<span class="comment">// Password input (characters hidden)</span>\n&lt;<span class="keyword">input</span> <span class="variable">type</span>=<span class="string">"password"</span> <span class="variable">name</span>=<span class="string">"password"</span>&gt;\n\n<span class="comment">// Email input (validates email format)</span>\n&lt;<span class="keyword">input</span> <span class="variable">type</span>=<span class="string">"email"</span> <span class="variable">name</span>=<span class="string">"email"</span>&gt;</code></pre>\n                </div>\n                \n                <h3>Common Input Attributes</h3>\n                <ul style="margin-left: 1.5rem; color: var(--text-gray);">\n                    <li><strong>name:</strong> Identifier for the data (required for form submission)</li>\n                    <li><strong>id:</strong> Unique identifier (links to label)</li>\n                    <li><strong>placeholder:</strong> Hint text shown when empty</li>\n                    <li><strong>value:</strong> Default/pre-filled value</li>\n                    <li><strong>required:</strong> Makes the field mandatory</li>\n                    <li><strong>disabled:</strong> Prevents user input</li>\n                    <li><strong>readonly:</strong> Visible but not editable</li>\n                    <li><strong>maxlength:</strong> Maximum character count</li>\n                </ul>\n            </section>\n\n            <!-- Section 3 -->\n            <section class="lesson-section">\n                <h2>Labels</h2>\n                <p>Labels are crucial for accessibility and usability:</p>\n                \n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code><span class="comment">// Method 1: Using for and id (preferred)</span>\n&lt;<span class="keyword">label</span> <span class="variable">for</span>=<span class="string">"email"</span>&gt;Email Address:&lt;/<span class="keyword">label</span>&gt;\n&lt;<span class="keyword">input</span> <span class="variable">type</span>=<span class="string">"email"</span> <span class="variable">id</span>=<span class="string">"email"</span> <span class="variable">name</span>=<span class="keyword">input</span> <span class="variable">type</span>=<span class="string">"email"</span> <span class="variable">name</span>=<span class="string">"email"</span>&gt;\n&lt;/<span class="keyword">label</span>&gt;</code></pre>\n                </div>\n                \n                <div class="tip-box">\n                    <svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg">\n                        <path d="M12 2C6.48 2 2 6.48 2 12s4.48 10 10 10 10-4.48 10-10S17.52 2 12 2zm1 15h-2v-6h2v6zm0-8h-2V7h2v2z"/>\n                    </svg>\n                    <p><strong>Why labels matter:</strong> Clicking a label focuses its input. Screen readers announce the label when the input is focused. Always use labels for accessibility!</p>\n                </div>\n            </section>\n\n            <!-- Section 4 -->\n            <section class="lesson-section">\n                <h2>Other  <span class="variable">placeholder</span>=<span class="string">"Type your message here..."</span>&gt;&lt;/<span class="keyword">textarea</span>&gt;\n\n<span class="comment">// rows: Height in Validation</h2>\n                <p>HTML5 provides built-in validation:</p>\n                \n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code>&lt;<span class="keyword">form</span>&gt;\n    <span class="comment">// Required field</span>\n    &lt;<span class="keyword">input</span> <span class="variable">type</span>=<span class="string">"text"</span> <span class="variable">name</span>=<span class="string">"name"</span> <span class="variable">required</span>&gt;\n    \n    <span class="comment">// Pattern matching (regex)</span>\n    &lt;<span class="variable">maxlength</span>=<span class="string">"20"</span>&gt;\n    \n    <span class="comment">// Min/max values</span>\n    &lt;<span class="keyword">input</span> <span class="variable">type</span>=<span class="string">"number"</span> <span class="variable">name</span>=<span class="string">"age"</span> <span class="variable">min</span>=<span class="string">"18"</span> <span class="variable">max</span>=<span class="string">"100"</span>&gt;\n    \n    &lt;<span class="keyword">button</span> <span class="variable">type</span>=<span class="string">"submit"</span>&gt;Submit&lt;/<span class="keyword">button</span>&gt;\n&lt;/<span class="keyword">form</span>&gt;</code></pre>\n                </div>\n            </section>\n\n            <!-- Section 10 -->\n            <section class="lesson-section">\n                <h2>Complete Form Example</h2>\n                \n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code>&lt;<span class="keyword">form</span> <span class="variable">action</span>=<span class="string">"/register"</span> <span class="variable">method</span>=<span       \n        &lt;<span class="keyword">label</span> <span class="variable">for</span>=<span class="string">"name"</span>&gt;Full Name:&lt;/<span class="keyword">label</span>&gt;\n        &lt;<span <h2>Key Takeaways</h2>\n                <div class="tip-box">\n                    <svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg">\n                        <path d="M12 2C6.48 2 2 6.48 2 12s4.48 10 10 10 10-4.48 10-10S17.52 2 12 2zm1 15h-2v-6h2v6zm0-8h-2V7h2v2z"/>\n                    </svg>\n                    <div>\n                        <p><strong>Remember:</strong></p>\n                        <ul style="margin-top: 0.5rem; margin-left: 1.5rem;">\n                            <li><strong>&lt;form&gt;:</strong> Container for form elements</li>\n                            <li><strong>&lt;input&gt;:</strong> Various input types (text, email, password, etc.)</li>\n                            <li><strong>&lt;label&gt;:</strong> Essential for accessibility</li>\n                            <li><strong>&lt;textarea&gt;:</strong> Multi-line text input</li>\n                            <li><strong>&lt;select&gt;/&lt;option&gt;:</strong> Dropdown menus</li>\n                            <li><strong>checkbox:</strong> Multiple selections allowed</li>\n                            <li><strong>radio:</strong> Single selection from group</li>\n                            <li><strong>required:</strong> Makes field mandatory</li>\n                            <li><strong>&lt;fieldset&gt;/&lt;legend&gt;:</strong> Group related form elements</li>\n                        </ul>\n                    </div>\n                </div>\n            </section>\n\n            <!-- Navigation -->\n            <div class="nav-buttons">\n                <a href="lesson5.html" Instead of using generic containers like &lt;div&gt; and &lt;span&gt; for everything, semantic elements describe what the content is.</p>\n                \n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code><span class="comment">// Non-semantic (doesn\'t describe content):</span>\n&lt;<span class="keyword">div</span> <span class="variable">class</span>=<span class="string">"header"</span>&gt;...&lt;/<span class="keyword">div</span>&gt;\n&lt;<span class="keyword">div</span> <span class="variable">class</span>=<span class="string">"nav"</span>&gt;...&lt;/<span class="keyword">div</span>&gt;\n&lt;<span class="keyword">div</span> <span class="variable">class</span>=<span class="string">"article"</span>&gt;...&lt;/<span class="keyword">div</span>&gt;\n&lt;<span class="keyword">div</span> <span class="variable">class</span>=<span class="string">"footer"</span>&gt;...&lt;/<span class="keyword">div</span>&gt;\n\n<span class="comment">// Semantic (describes content):</span>\n&lt;<span class="keyword">header</span>&gt;...&lt;/<span class="keyword">header</span>&gt;\n&lt;<span class="keyword">nav</span>&gt;...&lt;/<span class="keyword">nav</span>&gt;\n&lt;<span class="keyword">article</span>&gt;...&lt;/<span class="keyword">article</span>&gt;\n&lt;<span class="keyword">footer</span>&gt;...&lt;/<span class="keyword">footer</span>&gt;</code></pre>\n                </div>\n                \n                <div class="tip-box">\n                    <svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg">\n                        <path d="M12 2C6.48 2 2 6.48 2 12s4.48 10 10 10 10-4.48 10-10S17.52 2 12 2zm1 15h-2v-6h2v6zm0-8h-2V7h2v2z"/>\n                    </svg>\n                    <p><strong>Why semantics matter:</strong> They improve accessibility (screen readers understand the page structure), help SEO (search engines better understand content), and make code more readable and maintainable.</p>\n                </div>\n            </section>\n\n            <!-- Section 2 -->\n            <section class="lesson-section">\n                <h2>Page Structure Elements</h2>\n                \n                <h3>&lt;header&gt;</h3>\n                <p>Represents introductory content or navigational aids. Can be used for the page header or section headers.</p>\n                \n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code><span class="comment">// Page header</span>\n&lt;<span class="keyword">header</span>&gt;\n    &lt;<span class="keyword">h1</span>&gt;My Website&lt;/<span class="keyword">h1</span>&gt;\n    &lt;<span class="keyword">nav</span>&gt;...&lt;/<span class="keyword">nav</span>&gt;\n&lt;/<span class="keyword">header</span>&gt;\n\n<span class="comment">// Article header</span>\n&lt;<span class="keyword">article</span>&gt;\n    &lt;<span class="keyword">header</span>&gt;\n        &lt;<span class="keyword">h2</span>&gt;Article Title&lt;/<span class="keyword">h2</span>&gt;\n        &lt;<span class="keyword">time</span> <span class="variable">datetime</span>=<span class="string">"2024-01-15"</span>&gt;January 15, 2024&lt;/<span class="keyword">time</span>&gt;\n    &lt;/<span class="keyword">header</span>&gt;\n    &lt;<span class="keyword">p</span>&gt;Article content...&lt;/<span class="keyword">p</span>&gt;\n&lt;/<span class="keyword">article</span>&gt;</code></pre>\n                </div>\n                \n                <h3>&lt;nav&gt;</h3>\n                <p>Contains navigation links. Use for primary navigation, not for all link groups.</p>\n                \n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code>&lt;<span class="keyword">nav</span>&gt;\n    &lt;<span class="keyword">ul</span>&gt;\n        &lt;<span class="keyword">li</span>&gt;&lt;<span class="keyword">a</span> <span class="variable">href</span>=<span class="string">"/"</span>&gt;Home&lt;/<span class="keyword">a</span>&gt;&lt;/<span class="keyword">li</span>&gt;\n        &lt;<span class="keyword">li</span>&gt;&lt;<span class="keyword">a</span> <span class="variable">href</span>=<span class="string">"/about"</span>&gt;About&lt;/<span class="keyword">a</span>&gt;&lt;/<span class="keyword">li</span>&gt;\n        &lt;<span class="keyword">li</span>&gt;&lt;<span class="keyword">a</span> <span class="variable">href</span>=<span class="string">"/contact"</span>&gt;Contact&lt;/<span class="keyword">a</span>&gt;&lt;/<span class="keyword">li</span>&gt;\n    &lt;/<span class="keyword">ul</span>&gt;\n&lt;/<span class="keyword">nav</span>&gt;</code></pre>\n                </div>\n                \n                <h3>&lt;main&gt;</h3>\n                <p>Contains the main content of the page. There should be only one &lt;main&gt; per page.</p>\n                \n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code>&lt;<span class="keyword">main</span>&gt;\n    &lt;<span class="keyword">h1</span>&gt;Welcome to My Site&lt;/<span class="keyword">h1</span>&gt;\n    &lt;<span class="keyword">p</span>&gt;Main content goes here...&lt;/<span class="keyword">p</span>&gt;\n&lt;/<span class="keyword">main</span>&gt;\n\n<span class="comment">// Excludes: header, footer, nav, sidebars</span></code></pre>\n                </div>\n                \n                <h3>&lt;footer&gt;</h3>\n                <p>Contains footer content like copyright, contact info, or related links.</p>\n                \n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code>&lt;<span class="keyword">footer</span>&gt;\n    &lt;<span class="keyword">p</span>&gt;&copy; 2024 My Website. All rights reserved.&lt;/<span class="keyword">p</span>&gt;\n    &lt;<span class="keyword">nav</span>&gt;\n        &lt;<span class="keyword">a</span> <span class="variable">href</span>=<span class="string">"/privacy"</span>&gt;Privacy Policy&lt;/<span class="keyword">a</span>&gt;\n        &lt;<span class="keyword">a</span> <span class="variable">href</span>=<span class="string">"/terms"</span>&gt;Terms of Service&lt;/<span class="keyword">a</span>&gt;\n    &lt;/<span class="keyword">nav</span>&gt;\n&lt;/<span class="keyword">footer</span>&gt;</code></pre>\n                </div>\n            </section>\n\n            <!-- Section 3 -->\n            <section class="lesson-section">\n                <h2>Content Sectioning Elements</h2>\n                \n                <h3>&lt;section&gt;</h3>\n                <p>A thematic grouping of content, typically with a heading.</p>\n                \n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code>&lt;<span class="keyword">section</span>&gt;\n    &lt;<span class="keyword">h2</span>&gt;Our Services&lt;/<span class="keyword">h2</span>&gt;\n    &lt;<span class="keyword">p</span>&gt;We offer web development, design, and consulting.&lt;/<span class="keyword">p</span>&gt;\n&lt;/<span class="keyword">section</span>&gt;\n\n&lt;<span class="keyword">section</span>&gt;\n    &lt;<span class="keyword">h2</span>&gt;Contact Us&lt;/<span class="keyword">h2</span>&gt;\n    &lt;<span class="keyword">p</span>&gt;Email: hello@example.com&lt;/<span class="keyword">p</span>&gt;\n&lt;/<span class="keyword">section</span>&gt;</code></pre>\n                </div>\n                \n                <h3>&lt;article&gt;</h3>\n                <p>Self-contained content that could stand alone (blog post, news article, comment).</p>\n                \n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code>&lt;<span class="keyword">article</span>&gt;\n    &lt;<span class="keyword">header</span>&gt;\n        &lt;<span class="keyword">h2</span>&gt;How to Learn HTML&lt;/<span class="keyword">h2</span>&gt;\n        &lt;<span class="keyword">p</span>&gt;Posted on &lt;<span class="keyword">time</span> <span class="variable">datetime</span>=<span class="string">"2024-01-10"</span>&gt;January 10&lt;/<span class="keyword">time</span>&gt;&lt;/<span class="keyword">p</span>&gt;\n    &lt;/<span class="keyword">header</span>&gt;\n    &lt;<span class="keyword">p</span>&gt;HTML is the foundation of the web...&lt;/<span class="keyword">p</span>&gt;\n    &lt;<span class="keyword">footer</span>&gt;\n        &lt;<span class="keyword">p</span>&gt;Written by John Doe&lt;/<span class="keyword">p</span>&gt;\n    &lt;/<span class="keyword">footer</span>&gt;\n&lt;/<span class="keyword">article</span>&gt;</code></pre>\n                </div>\n                \n                <div class="code-explanation">\n                    <p><strong>Section vs Article:</strong> An article is self-contained and could be syndicated (like a blog post). A section is a thematic grouping within a page. Both typically have headings.</p>\n                </div>\n                \n                <h3>&lt;aside&gt;</h3>\n                <p>Content tangentially related to the main content (sidebars, pull quotes).</p>\n                \n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code>&lt;<span class="keyword">aside</span>&gt;\n    &lt;<span class="keyword">h3</span>&gt;Related Articles&lt;/<span class="keyword">h3</span>&gt;\n    &lt;<span class="keyword">ul</span>&gt;\n        &lt;<span class="keyword">li</span>&gt;&lt;<span class="keyword">a</span> <span class="variable">href</span>=<span class="string">"#"</span>&gt;CSS Basics&lt;/<span class="keyword">a</span>&gt;&lt;/<span class="keyword">li</span>&gt;\n        &lt;<span class="keyword">li</span>&gt;&lt;<span class="keyword">a</span> <span class="variable">href</span>=<span class="string">"#"</span>&gt;JavaScript Introduction&lt;/<span class="keyword">a</span>&gt;&lt;/<span class="keyword">li</span>&gt;\n    &lt;/<span class="keyword">ul</span>&gt;\n&lt;/<span class="keyword">aside</span>&gt;</code></pre>\n                </div>\n            </section>\n\n            <!-- Section 4 -->\n            <section class="lesson-section">\n                <h2>Complete Page Layout Example</h2>\n                \n                <div &lt;/<span class="keyword">ul</span>&gt;\n        &lt;/<span class="keyword">nav</span>&gt;\n    &lt;/<span class="keyword">header</span>&gt;\n\n    &lt;<span class="keyword">main</span>&gt;\n        &lt;<span class="keyword">article</span>&gt;\n            &lt;<span class="keyword">header</span>&gt;\n                &lt;<span class="keyword">h2</span>&gt;My First Blog Post&lt;/<span &lt;/<span class="keyword">ul</span>&gt;\n        &lt;/<span class="keyword">aside</span>&gt;\n    &lt;/<span class="keyword">main</span>&gt;\n\n    &lt;<span class="keyword">footer</span>&gt;\n        &lt;<span class="keyword">p</span>&gt;&copy; 2024 My Blog&lt;/<span class="keyword">p</span>&gt;\n    &lt;/<span class="keyword">footer</span>&gt;\n&lt;/<span class="keyword">body</span>&gt;</code></pre>\n                </div>\n            </section>\n\n            <!-- Section 5 -->\n            <section class="lesson-section">\n                <h2>Other Semantic Elements</h2>\n                \n                <h3>&lt;figure&gt; and &lt;figcaption&gt;</h3>\n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code>&lt;<span <pre><code><span class="comment">// Machine-readable datetime</span>\n&lt;<span class="keyword">time</span> <span class="variable">datetime</span>=<span class="string">"2024-01-15"</span>&gt;January 15, 2024&lt;/<span class="keyword">time</span>&gt;\n\n<spanspan class="comment">// Time with timezone</span>\n&lt;<span class="keyword">time</span> <span class="variable">datetime</span>=<span class="variable">datetime</span>=<span class="string">"PT2H30M"</span>&gt;2 hours 30 minutes&lt;/<span class="keyword">time</span>&gt;</code></pre>\n                </div>\n                \n                <h3>&lt;address&gt;</h3>\n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code>&lt;<span class="keyword">address</span>&gt;\n    Written by &lt;<span class="keyword">a</span> <span class="variable">href</span>=<span class="string">"mailto:john@example.com"</span>&gt;John Doe&lt;/<span class="keyword">a</span>&gt;&lt;<span class="keyword">br</span>&gt;\n    Visit us at: &lt;<span class="keyword">a</span> <span class="variable">href</span>=<span class="string">"https://example.com"</span>&gt;example.com&lt;/<span class="keyword">a</span>&gt;&lt;<span class="keyword">br</span>&gt;\n    123 Main Street, New York, NY\n&lt;/<span class="keyword">address</span>&gt;</code></pre>\n                </div>\n                \n                <h3>&lt;details&gt; and &lt;summary&gt;</h3>\n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code>&lt;<span class="keyword">details</span>&gt;\n    &lt;<span class="variable">open</span>&gt;\n    &lt;<span class="keyword">summary</span>&gt;FAQ: What is HTML?&lt;/<span class="keyword">summary</span>&gt;\n    &lt;<span class="keyword">p</span>&gt;HTML stands for HyperText Markup Language...&lt;/<span class="keyword">p</span>&gt;\n&lt;/<span class="keyword">details</span>&gt;</code></pre>\n                </div>\n            </section>\n\n            <!-- Section 6 -->\n            <section class="lesson-section">\n                <h2>Text-Level Semantics</h2>\n                \n                <h3>&lt;mark&gt;</h3>\n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code>&lt;<span class="keyword">p</span>&gt;Search results for "HTML": &lt;<span class="keyword">mark</span>&gt;HTML&lt;/<span class="keyword">mark</span>&gt; is the standard markup language...&lt;/<span class="keyword">p</span>&gt;</code></pre>\n                </div>\n                \n                <h3>&lt;cite&gt;</h3>\n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code>&lt;<span class="keyword">p</span>&gt;&lt;<span class="keyword">cite</span>&gt;The Art of Programming&lt;/<span class="keyword">cite</span>&gt; by John Smith is a great book.&lt;/<span class="keyword">p</span>&gt;</code></pre>\n                </div>\n                \n                <h3>&lt;abbr&gt;</h3>\n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code>&lt;<span class="keyword">p</span>&gt;I work with &lt;<span class="keyword">abbr</span> <span class="variable">title</span>=<span class="string">"HyperText Markup Language"</span>&gt;HTML&lt;/<span class="keyword">abbr</span>&gt; every day.&lt;/<span class="keyword">p</span>&gt;</code></pre>\n                </div>\n            </section>\n\n            <!-- Key Takeaways -->\n            <section class="lesson-section">\n                <h2>Key Takeaways</h2>\n                <div class="tip-box">\n                    <svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg">\n                        <path d="M12 2C6.48 2 2 6.48 2 12s4.48 10 10 10 10-4.48 10-10S17.52 2 12 2zm1 15h-2v-6h2v6zm0-8h-2V7h2v2z"/>\n                    </svg>\n                    <div>\n                        <p><strong>Remember:</strong></p>\n                        <ul style="margin-top: 0.5rem; margin-left: 1.5rem;">\n                            <li><strong>&lt;header&gt;:</strong> Introductory content or navigation</li>\n                            <li><strong>&lt;nav&gt;:</strong> Navigation links</li>\n                            <li><strong>&lt;main&gt;:</strong> Main content (one per page)</li>\n                            <li><strong>&lt;article&gt;:</strong> Self-contained content</li>\n                            <li><strong>&lt;section&gt;:</strong> Thematic grouping of content</li>\n                            <li><strong>&lt;aside&gt;:</strong> Related but separate content</li>\n                            <li><strong>&lt;footer&gt;:</strong> Footer content</li>\n                            <li><strong>&lt;figure&gt;:</strong> Self-contained content like images</li>\n                            <li><strong>&lt;time&gt;:</strong> Machine-readable dates/times</li>\n                            <li><strong>Benefits:</strong> Better accessibility, SEO, and <li><strong>class:</strong> Reusable identifier (many per page)</li>\n                            <li><strong>style:</strong> Inline CSS (use sparingly)</li>\n
